\DoxyCodeLine{00569\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ of\ up\ to\ 23\ chars\ on\ the\ stack\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/\ the\ last\ byte\ of\ the\ buffer\ is\ used\ for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00570\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ -\/\ the\ highest\ bit\ -\/\ if\ "{}0"{}\ then\ it\ is\ small\ -\/\ otherwise\ its\ "{}1"{}\ (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00571\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ capacity\ left\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/\ using\ the\ lowest\ 5\ bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00572\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ 2\ bits\ are\ left\ unused\ -\/\ the\ second\ and\ third\ highest\ ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00573\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ acts\ as\ a\ null\ terminator\ if\ strlen()\ is\ 23\ (24\ including\ the\ null\ terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00574\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ the\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ remains\ "{}0"{}\ ("{}as\ well\ as\ the\ capacity\ left"{})\ so\ its\ OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00575\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Idea\ taken\ from\ this\ lecture\ about\ the\ string\ implementation\ of\ facebook/folly\ -\/\ fbstring}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03434\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ store.\ Instead\ of\ using\ a\ single\ atomic\ variable,\ this\ splits\ up\ into\ multiple\ ones,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03435\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ each\ sitting\ on\ a\ separate\ cache\ line.\ The\ goal\ is\ to\ provide\ a\ speedup\ when\ most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03436\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ operations\ are\ modifying.\ It\ achieves\ this\ with\ two\ properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03437\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03438\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *\ Multiple\ atomics\ are\ used,\ so\ chance\ of\ congestion\ from\ the\ same\ atomic\ is\ reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03439\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *\ Each\ atomic\ sits\ on\ a\ separate\ cache\ line,\ so\ false\ sharing\ is\ reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03440\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03441\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ disadvantage\ is\ that\ there\ is\ a\ small\ overhead\ due\ to\ the\ use\ of\ TLS,\ and\ load/store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03442\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ slower\ because\ all\ atomics\ have\ to\ be\ accessed.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03493\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Each\ thread\ has\ a\ different\ atomic\ that\ it\ operates\ on.\ If\ more\ than\ NumLanes\ threads}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03495\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ everything\ will\ work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03496\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03497\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ logic\ here\ is\ a\ bit\ tricky.\ The\ call\ should\ be\ as\ fast\ as\ possible,\ so\ that\ there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03498\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ minimal\ to\ no\ overhead\ in\ determining\ the\ correct\ atomic\ for\ the\ current\ thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03499\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03500\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 1.\ A\ global\ static\ counter\ laneCounter\ counts\ continuously\ up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03501\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 2.\ Each\ successive\ thread\ will\ use\ modulo\ operation\ of\ that\ counter\ so\ it\ gets\ an\ atomic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03502\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ assigned\ in\ a\ round-\/robin\ fashion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03503\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 3.\ This\ tlsLaneIdx\ is\ stored\ in\ the\ thread\ local\ data,\ so\ it\ is\ directly\ available\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03504\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ little\ overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03505\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Atomic<T>\&\ myAtomic()\ \mbox{\hyperlink{doctest_8h_a0a3c492342c533baad7b21af7903e6b4}{DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT}}\ \{}
